<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">Shades of green</h1> <div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
<div class="noprint" id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div> <div id="contentSub"></div>
<div id="jump-to-nav"></div> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a>
<div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">"Gray-green" redirects here. For the bus operator, see <a href="/wiki/Grey-Green" title="Grey-Green">Grey-Green</a>.</div>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">For a broader coverage of this topic, see <a href="/wiki/Green" title="Green">Green</a>.</div>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold">Green</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">

~575–525 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Terahertz_(unit)" title="Terahertz (unit)">THz</a></td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><span style="position: relative; float: right; font-size: 70%"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Color/Normalized_Color_Coordinates" title="About these coordinates"><img alt="About these coordinates" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="60" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/15px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/23px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/30px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 2x" width="15"/></a></span>     Color coordinates</th></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/SRGB_color_space" title="SRGB color space">sRGB</a><sup><b>B</b></sup>  (<a href="/wiki/Red" title="Red">r</a>, <a href="/wiki/Green" title="Green">g</a>, <a href="/wiki/Blue" title="Blue">b</a>)</th><td>
(0, 128, 0)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HSV_color_space" title="HSV color space">HSV</a>       (<a href="/wiki/Hue" title="Hue">h</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saturation_(color_theory)" title="Saturation (color theory)">s</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brightness" title="Brightness">v</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(120°, 100%, 50%)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Source</th><td>
W3C TR CSS3 Color Module<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-css3-color_1-0"><a href="#cite_note-css3-color-1">[1]</a></sup></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
Some tints and shades of green</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>Varieties of the <a href="/wiki/Color" title="Color">color</a> <a href="/wiki/Green" title="Green">green</a> may differ in <a href="/wiki/Hue" title="Hue">hue</a>, <a href="/wiki/Colorfulness" title="Colorfulness">chroma</a> (also called saturation or intensity) or <a href="/wiki/Lightness" title="Lightness">lightness</a> (or value, tone, or <a href="/wiki/Brightness" title="Brightness">brightness</a>), or in two or three of these qualities. Variations in value are also called <a href="/wiki/Tints_and_shades" title="Tints and shades">tints and shades</a>, a tint being a green or other hue mixed with white, a shade being mixed with black. A large selection of these various colors is shown below.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Green_Moray_Eel_(Gymnothorax_funebris),_Cozumel.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2020" data-file-width="2694" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Green_Moray_Eel_%28Gymnothorax_funebris%29%2C_Cozumel.jpg/200px-Green_Moray_Eel_%28Gymnothorax_funebris%29%2C_Cozumel.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Green_Moray_Eel_%28Gymnothorax_funebris%29%2C_Cozumel.jpg/300px-Green_Moray_Eel_%28Gymnothorax_funebris%29%2C_Cozumel.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Green_Moray_Eel_%28Gymnothorax_funebris%29%2C_Cozumel.jpg/400px-Green_Moray_Eel_%28Gymnothorax_funebris%29%2C_Cozumel.jpg 2x" width="200"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Green_Moray_Eel_(Gymnothorax_funebris),_Cozumel.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Green Moray eel (Gymnothorax funebris)</div></div></div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Green_in_nature">Green in nature</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Green in nature">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Green#In_biology" title="Green">Green § In biology</a></div>
<p>Green is common in nature, especially in plants. Many plants are green mainly because of a complex chemical known as <a href="/wiki/Chlorophyll" title="Chlorophyll">chlorophyll</a> which is involved in <a href="/wiki/Photosynthesis" title="Photosynthesis">photosynthesis</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-brit_2-0"><a href="#cite_note-brit-2">[2]</a></sup> Many shades of green have been named after plants or are related to plants. Due to varying ratios of chlorophylls (and different amounts as well as other plant pigments being present), the plant kingdom exhibits many shades of green in both hue (true color) and value (lightness/darkness). The chlorophylls in living plants have distinctive green colors, while dried or cooked portions of plants are different shades of green due to the chlorophyll molecules losing their inner magnesium ion.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Artichoke">Artichoke</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Artichoke">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:142px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:P8220094--CroppedImage.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1785" data-file-width="1352" height="185" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/86/P8220094--CroppedImage.jpg/140px-P8220094--CroppedImage.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/86/P8220094--CroppedImage.jpg/210px-P8220094--CroppedImage.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/86/P8220094--CroppedImage.jpg/280px-P8220094--CroppedImage.jpg 2x" width="140"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:P8220094--CroppedImage.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>An <a href="/wiki/Artichoke" title="Artichoke">artichoke</a></div></div></div>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold">Artichoke</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;line-height:12px; background-color:#8F9779; border: 0.1px solid #000000">
 </td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><span style="position: relative; float: right; font-size: 70%"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Color/Normalized_Color_Coordinates" title="About these coordinates"><img alt="About these coordinates" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="60" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/15px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/23px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/30px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 2x" width="15"/></a></span>     Color coordinates</th></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Web_colors#Hex_triplet" title="Web colors">Hex triplet</a></th><td>

(143, 151, 121)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/CMYK_color_model" title="CMYK color model">CMYK</a><sup><b>H</b></sup>   (<a href="/wiki/Cyan" title="Cyan">c</a>, <a href="/wiki/Magenta" title="Magenta">m</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yellow" title="Yellow">y</a>, <a href="/wiki/Black" title="Black">k</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(5, 0, 20, 41)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HSV_color_space" title="HSV color space">HSV</a>       (<a href="/wiki/Hue" title="Hue">h</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saturation_(color_theory)" title="Saturation (color theory)">s</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brightness" title="Brightness">v</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(76°, 20%, 59%)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Source</th><td>
<a class="external text" href="http://tx4.us/nbs/nbs-a.htm" rel="nofollow">ISCC NBS</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/><b>H</b>: Normalized to [0–100] (hundred)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><i>Artichoke</i> is a color that is a representation of the color of a raw fresh uncooked <a href="/wiki/Artichoke" title="Artichoke">artichoke</a>. Another name for this color is <i>artichoke green</i>.
</p><p>The first recorded use of "artichoke green" as a color name in <a href="/wiki/English_language" title="English language">English</a> was in 1905.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup>
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>

<p>This is the color called <i>artichoke green</i> in <a href="/wiki/Pantone" title="Pantone">Pantone</a>. The source is Pantone 18-0125 TPX<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup>
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Asparagus">Asparagus</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Asparagus">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold">Asparagus</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;line-height:12px; background-color:#87A96B; border: 0.1px solid #000000">
 </td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><span style="position: relative; float: right; font-size: 70%"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Color/Normalized_Color_Coordinates" title="About these coordinates"><img alt="About these coordinates" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="60" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/15px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/23px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/30px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 2x" width="15"/></a></span>     Color coordinates</th></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Web_colors#Hex_triplet" title="Web colors">Hex triplet</a></th><td>
#87A96B</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/SRGB_color_space" title="SRGB color space">sRGB</a><sup><b>B</b></sup>  (<a href="/wiki/Red" title="Red">r</a>, <a href="/wiki/Green" title="Green">g</a>, <a href="/wiki/Blue" title="Blue">b</a>)</th><td>
(135, 169, 107)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/CMYK_color_model" title="CMYK color model">CMYK</a><sup><b>H</b></sup>   (<a href="/wiki/Cyan" title="Cyan">c</a>, <a href="/wiki/Magenta" title="Magenta">m</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yellow" title="Yellow">y</a>, <a href="/wiki/Black" title="Black">k</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(20, 0, 37, 34)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HSV_color_space" title="HSV color space">HSV</a>       (<a href="/wiki/Hue" title="Hue">h</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saturation_(color_theory)" title="Saturation (color theory)">s</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brightness" title="Brightness">v</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(93°, 37%, 66%)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Source</th><td>
<a href="/wiki/List_of_Crayola_crayon_colors" title="List of Crayola crayon colors">Crayola</a></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/><b>H</b>: Normalized to [0–100] (hundred)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><i>Asparagus</i> is a tone of green that is named after the <a href="/wiki/Asparagus" title="Asparagus">vegetable</a>. <a href="/wiki/Crayola" title="Crayola">Crayola</a> created this color in 1993 as one of the 16 to be named in the Name the Color Contest.
</p><p>It is also the color of a wild asparagus plant blowing in the wind of the 1949 classic film <i><a href="/wiki/Sands_of_Iwo_Jima" title="Sands of Iwo Jima">Sands of Iwo Jima</a></i>.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Asparagus_image.jpg"><img alt="Bundled stalks of asparagus" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1200" data-file-width="1600" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/Asparagus_image.jpg/220px-Asparagus_image.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/Asparagus_image.jpg/330px-Asparagus_image.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/Asparagus_image.jpg/440px-Asparagus_image.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Asparagus_image.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Bundled stalks of asparagus</div></div></div>
<p>Another name for this color is <i>asparagus green</i>. The first recorded use of "asparagus green" as a color name in English was in 1805.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup>
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Avocado">Avocado</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Avocado">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Chartreuse_(color)#Avocado" title="Chartreuse (color)">Chartreuse_(color) § Avocado</a></div>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:188px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Avocado.jpeg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="200" data-file-width="186" height="200" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/1/1d/Avocado.jpeg" width="186"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Avocado.jpeg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>An <a href="/wiki/Avocado" title="Avocado">avocado</a></div></div></div>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold">Avocado</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;line-height:12px; background-color:#568203; border: 0.1px solid #000000">
 </td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><span style="position: relative; float: right; font-size: 70%"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Color/Normalized_Color_Coordinates" title="About these coordinates"><img alt="About these coordinates" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="60" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/15px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/23px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/30px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 2x" width="15"/></a></span>     Color coordinates</th></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Web_colors#Hex_triplet" title="Web colors">Hex triplet</a></th><td>
#568203</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/SRGB_color_space" title="SRGB color space">sRGB</a><sup><b>B</b></sup>  (<a href="/wiki/Red" title="Red">r</a>, <a href="/wiki/Green" title="Green">g</a>, <a href="/wiki/Blue" title="Blue">b</a>)</th><td>
(86, 130, 3)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/CMYK_color_model" title="CMYK color model">CMYK</a><sup><b>H</b></sup>   (<a href="/wiki/Cyan" title="Cyan">c</a>, <a href="/wiki/Magenta" title="Magenta">m</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yellow" title="Yellow">y</a>, <a href="/wiki/Black" title="Black">k</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(34, 0, 98, 49)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HSV_color_space" title="HSV color space">HSV</a>       (<a href="/wiki/Hue" title="Hue">h</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saturation_(color_theory)" title="Saturation (color theory)">s</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brightness" title="Brightness">v</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(81°, 98%, 51%)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Source</th><td>
<a class="external text" href="http://pourpre.com/chroma/dico.php?typ=teinte&amp;ent=80" rel="nofollow">Pourpre.com</a></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/><b>H</b>: Normalized to [0–100] (hundred)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><i>Avocado</i> is a color that is a representation of the color of the outer surface of an <a href="/wiki/Avocado" title="Avocado">avocado</a>.
</p><p>The color avocado is a dark yellow-green color.
</p><p>Avocado was a common color for metal surfaces (including <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Automobiles" title="Automobiles">automobiles</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Household_appliances" title="Household appliances">household appliances</a>), as well as the color <a href="/wiki/Gold_(color)#Harvest_gold" title="Gold (color)">harvest gold</a>, during the whole decade of the 1970s. They were both also popular colors for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Shag_carpet" title="Shag carpet">shag carpets</a>. Both colors went out of style by the early 1980s.
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dark_green">Dark green</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Dark green">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

#013220</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/SRGB_color_space" title="SRGB color space">sRGB</a><sup><b>B</b></sup>  (<a href="/wiki/Red" title="Red">r</a>, <a href="/wiki/Green" title="Green">g</a>, <a href="/wiki/Blue" title="Blue">b</a>)</th><td>
(1, 50, 32)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/CMYK_color_model" title="CMYK color model">CMYK</a><sup><b>H</b></sup>   (<a href="/wiki/Cyan" title="Cyan">c</a>, <a href="/wiki/Magenta" title="Magenta">m</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yellow" title="Yellow">y</a>, <a href="/wiki/Black" title="Black">k</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(98, 0, 36, 80)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HSV_color_space" title="HSV color space">HSV</a>       (<a href="/wiki/Hue" title="Hue">h</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saturation_(color_theory)" title="Saturation (color theory)">s</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brightness" title="Brightness">v</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(158°, 98%, %)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Source</th><td>

<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/><b>H</b>: Normalized to [0–100] (hundred)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><i>Dark green</i> is a dark shade of green. A different shade of green has been designated as "<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dark_green_(X11)" title="Dark green (X11)">dark green (X11)</a>" for certain computer uses.
</p>

<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/><b>H</b>: Normalized to [0–100] (hundred)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><i>Fern green</i> is a color that resembles <a href="/wiki/Fern" title="Fern">ferns</a>. A <a href="/wiki/List_of_Crayola_crayon_colors" title="List of Crayola crayon colors">Crayola crayon</a> named <i>fern</i> was created in 1998, which is a lighter shade of the top color shown on the right.
</p><p>The first recorded use of <i>fern green</i> as a color name in English was in 1902.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup>
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Forest_green">Forest green</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Forest green">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Forest_green" title="Forest green">Forest green</a></div>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold">Forest green</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;line-height:12px; background-color:#228B22; border: 0.1px solid #000000">
 </td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><span style="position: relative; float: right; font-size: 70%"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Color/Normalized_Color_Coordinates" title="About these coordinates"><img alt="About these coordinates" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="60" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/15px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/23px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/30px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 2x" width="15"/></a></span>     Color coordinates</th></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Web_colors#Hex_triplet" title="Web colors">Hex triplet</a></th><td>

(34, 139, 34)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/CMYK_color_model" title="CMYK color model">CMYK</a><sup><b>H</b></sup>   (<a href="/wiki/Cyan" title="Cyan">c</a>, <a href="/wiki/Magenta" title="Magenta">m</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yellow" title="Yellow">y</a>, <a href="/wiki/Black" title="Black">k</a>)</span></th><td>

<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/><b>H</b>: Normalized to [0–100] (hundred)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Ivy_in_Hyde_Park.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3000" data-file-width="4000" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Ivy_in_Hyde_Park.JPG/220px-Ivy_in_Hyde_Park.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Ivy_in_Hyde_Park.JPG/330px-Ivy_in_Hyde_Park.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Ivy_in_Hyde_Park.JPG/440px-Ivy_in_Hyde_Park.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Ivy_in_Hyde_Park.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Hedera" title="Hedera">Hedera</a> in <a href="/wiki/Hyde_Park,_Sydney" title="Hyde Park, Sydney">Hyde Park, Sydney</a></div></div></div>
<p><i>Forest green</i> refers to a green color said to resemble the color of the trees and other plants in a <a href="/wiki/Forest" title="Forest">forest</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup>
</p><p>The first recorded use of <i>forest green</i> as the name of a color in the English language was in 1810.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup>
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>

<h3><span id="Hooker.27s_green"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Hooker's_green">Hooker's green</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Hooker's green">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold">Hooker's green</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;line-height:12px; background-color:#49796B; border: 0.1px solid #000000">
 </td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><span style="position: relative; float: right; font-size: 70%"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Color/Normalized_Color_Coordinates" title="About these coordinates"><img alt="About these coordinates" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="60" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/15px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/23px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/30px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 2x" width="15"/></a></span>     Color coordinates</th></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Web_colors#Hex_triplet" title="Web colors">Hex triplet</a></th><td>
#49796B</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/SRGB_color_space" title="SRGB color space">sRGB</a><sup><b>B</b></sup>  (<a href="/wiki/Red" title="Red">r</a>, <a href="/wiki/Green" title="Green">g</a>, <a href="/wiki/Blue" title="Blue">b</a>)</th><td>
(73, 121, 107)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/CMYK_color_model" title="CMYK color model">CMYK</a><sup><b>H</b></sup>   (<a href="/wiki/Cyan" title="Cyan">c</a>, <a href="/wiki/Magenta" title="Magenta">m</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yellow" title="Yellow">y</a>, <a href="/wiki/Black" title="Black">k</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(73, 36, 59, 15)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HSV_color_space" title="HSV color space">HSV</a>       (<a href="/wiki/Hue" title="Hue">h</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saturation_(color_theory)" title="Saturation (color theory)">s</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brightness" title="Brightness">v</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(163°, 39.7%, 47.5%)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Source</th><td>
<a class="external text" href="http://www.winsornewton.com/products/acrylic-colours/galeria-acrylic-colour/colour-chart/" rel="nofollow">Winsor &amp; Newton</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-hookers-green-color_12-0"><a href="#cite_note-hookers-green-color-12">[12]</a></sup></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/><b>H</b>: Normalized to [0–100] (hundred)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><i>Hooker's green</i> is a dark green color created by mixing <a href="/wiki/Prussian_blue" title="Prussian blue">Prussian blue</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gamboge" title="Gamboge">Gamboge</a>. It is displayed on the right.
</p><p>Hooker's green takes its name from botanical artist <a href="/wiki/William_Hooker_(botanical_illustrator)" title="William Hooker (botanical illustrator)">William Hooker</a> (1779–1832) who first created a special pigment for leaves.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup>
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Jungle_green">Jungle green</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Jungle green">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Jungle_green" title="Jungle green">Jungle green</a></div>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold">Jungle green</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;line-height:12px; background-color:#29AB87; border: 0.1px solid #000000">
 </td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><span style="position: relative; float: right; font-size: 70%"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Color/Normalized_Color_Coordinates" title="About these coordinates"><img alt="About these coordinates" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="60" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/15px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/23px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/30px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 2x" width="15"/></a></span>     Color coordinates</th></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Web_colors#Hex_triplet" title="Web colors">Hex triplet</a></th><td>
#29AB87</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/SRGB_color_space" title="SRGB color space">sRGB</a><sup><b>B</b></sup>  (<a href="/wiki/Red" title="Red">r</a>, <a href="/wiki/Green" title="Green">g</a>, <a href="/wiki/Blue" title="Blue">b</a>)</th><td>
(41, 171, 135)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/CMYK_color_model" title="CMYK color model">CMYK</a><sup><b>H</b></sup>   (<a href="/wiki/Cyan" title="Cyan">c</a>, <a href="/wiki/Magenta" title="Magenta">m</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yellow" title="Yellow">y</a>, <a href="/wiki/Black" title="Black">k</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(50, 0, 50, 2)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HSV_color_space" title="HSV color space">HSV</a>       (<a href="/wiki/Hue" title="Hue">h</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saturation_(color_theory)" title="Saturation (color theory)">s</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brightness" title="Brightness">v</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(120°, 80%, 70%)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Source</th><td>
Crayola</td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/><b>H</b>: Normalized to [0–100] (hundred)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>Displayed at right is the color <i>jungle green</i>. In 1990, Crayola named and formulated this specific tone of jungle green.
</p><p>The first recorded use of <i>jungle green</i> as a name of a color in the English language was in 1926.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup>
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Laurel_green">Laurel green</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Laurel green">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold">Laurel green</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;line-height:12px; background-color:#A9BA9D; border: 0.1px solid #000000">
 </td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><span style="position: relative; float: right; font-size: 70%"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Color/Normalized_Color_Coordinates" title="About these coordinates"><img alt="About these coordinates" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="60" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/15px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/23px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/30px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 2x" width="15"/></a></span>     Color coordinates</th></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Web_colors#Hex_triplet" title="Web colors">Hex triplet</a></th><td>
#A9BA9D</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/SRGB_color_space" title="SRGB color space">sRGB</a><sup><b>B</b></sup>  (<a href="/wiki/Red" title="Red">r</a>, <a href="/wiki/Green" title="Green">g</a>, <a href="/wiki/Blue" title="Blue">b</a>)</th><td>
(169, 186, 157)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/CMYK_color_model" title="CMYK color model">CMYK</a><sup><b>H</b></sup>   (<a href="/wiki/Cyan" title="Cyan">c</a>, <a href="/wiki/Magenta" title="Magenta">m</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yellow" title="Yellow">y</a>, <a href="/wiki/Black" title="Black">k</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(9, 0, 16, 27)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HSV_color_space" title="HSV color space">HSV</a>       (<a href="/wiki/Hue" title="Hue">h</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saturation_(color_theory)" title="Saturation (color theory)">s</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brightness" title="Brightness">v</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(95°, 16%, 73%)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Source</th><td>
Maerz and Paul<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/><b>H</b>: Normalized to [0–100] (hundred)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><i>Laurel green</i> is a medium light hue of greenish gray similar to asparagus, but lighter.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:LaurelwreathDK.JPG"><img alt="A laurel wreath" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1984" data-file-width="1704" height="256" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/LaurelwreathDK.JPG/220px-LaurelwreathDK.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/LaurelwreathDK.JPG/330px-LaurelwreathDK.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/LaurelwreathDK.JPG/440px-LaurelwreathDK.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:LaurelwreathDK.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>A <a href="/wiki/Laurel_wreath" title="Laurel wreath">laurel wreath</a></div></div></div>
<p>The first recorded use of <i>laurel green</i> as a name of a color in the English language was in 1705.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup>
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Light_green">Light green</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Light green">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<p><i>Light green</i> is a light tint of green.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mantis">Mantis</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Mantis">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Mantis_religiosa_MHNT_enti%C3%A8re.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="4912" data-file-width="7047" height="139" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/57/Mantis_religiosa_MHNT_enti%C3%A8re.jpg/200px-Mantis_religiosa_MHNT_enti%C3%A8re.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/57/Mantis_religiosa_MHNT_enti%C3%A8re.jpg/300px-Mantis_religiosa_MHNT_enti%C3%A8re.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/57/Mantis_religiosa_MHNT_enti%C3%A8re.jpg/400px-Mantis_religiosa_MHNT_enti%C3%A8re.jpg 2x" width="200"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Mantis_religiosa_MHNT_enti%C3%A8re.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Praying_mantis" title="Praying mantis">praying mantis</a></div></div></div>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold">Mantis</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;line-height:12px; background-color:#74C365; border: 0.1px solid #000000">
 </td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><span style="position: relative; float: right; font-size: 70%"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Color/Normalized_Color_Coordinates" title="About these coordinates"><img alt="About these coordinates" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="60" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/15px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/23px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/30px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 2x" width="15"/></a></span>     Color coordinates</th></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Web_colors#Hex_triplet" title="Web colors">Hex triplet</a></th><td>
#74C365</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/SRGB_color_space" title="SRGB color space">sRGB</a><sup><b>B</b></sup>  (<a href="/wiki/Red" title="Red">r</a>, <a href="/wiki/Green" title="Green">g</a>, <a href="/wiki/Blue" title="Blue">b</a>)</th><td>
(116, 195, 101)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/CMYK_color_model" title="CMYK color model">CMYK</a><sup><b>H</b></sup>   (<a href="/wiki/Cyan" title="Cyan">c</a>, <a href="/wiki/Magenta" title="Magenta">m</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yellow" title="Yellow">y</a>, <a href="/wiki/Black" title="Black">k</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(41, 0, 48, 24)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HSV_color_space" title="HSV color space">HSV</a>       (<a href="/wiki/Hue" title="Hue">h</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saturation_(color_theory)" title="Saturation (color theory)">s</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brightness" title="Brightness">v</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(110°, 48%, 77%)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Source</th><td>
<a class="external text" href="http://xona.com/colorlist/" rel="nofollow">Xona.com color list</a></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/><b>H</b>: Normalized to [0–100] (hundred)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><i>Mantis</i> is a color that is a representation of the color of a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Praying_mantis" title="Praying mantis">praying mantis</a>.
</p><p>The first use of <i>mantis</i> as a color name in English was when it was included as one of the colors on the Xona.com color list, promulgated in 2001.
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mint_green">Mint green</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Mint green">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold">Mint green</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;line-height:12px; background-color:#98FB98; border: 0.1px solid #000000">
 </td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><span style="position: relative; float: right; font-size: 70%"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Color/Normalized_Color_Coordinates" title="About these coordinates"><img alt="About these coordinates" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="60" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/15px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/23px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/30px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 2x" width="15"/></a></span>     Color coordinates</th></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Web_colors#Hex_triplet" title="Web colors">Hex triplet</a></th><td>

(152, 251, 152)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/CMYK_color_model" title="CMYK color model">CMYK</a><sup><b>H</b></sup>   (<a href="/wiki/Cyan" title="Cyan">c</a>, <a href="/wiki/Magenta" title="Magenta">m</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yellow" title="Yellow">y</a>, <a href="/wiki/Black" title="Black">k</a>)</span></th><td>

<span class="nowrap">(120°, 39%, 98%)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Source</th><td>
<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_HTML_color_names" title="List of HTML color names">X11</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-css3-color_1-2"><a href="#cite_note-css3-color-1">[1]</a></sup></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/><b>H</b>: Normalized to [0–100] (hundred)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><i>Mint green</i> is a pale tint of green that resembles the color of mint green pigment, and was a popular color in the 1950s, and 1990s. This is also known as Pale Green.
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Moss_green">Moss green</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Moss green">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Moss-covered_grave,_St._Mary%27s,_Newent._-_geograph.org.uk_-_526488.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="640" data-file-width="608" height="232" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a8/Moss-covered_grave%2C_St._Mary%27s%2C_Newent._-_geograph.org.uk_-_526488.jpg/220px-Moss-covered_grave%2C_St._Mary%27s%2C_Newent._-_geograph.org.uk_-_526488.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a8/Moss-covered_grave%2C_St._Mary%27s%2C_Newent._-_geograph.org.uk_-_526488.jpg/330px-Moss-covered_grave%2C_St._Mary%27s%2C_Newent._-_geograph.org.uk_-_526488.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a8/Moss-covered_grave%2C_St._Mary%27s%2C_Newent._-_geograph.org.uk_-_526488.jpg/440px-Moss-covered_grave%2C_St._Mary%27s%2C_Newent._-_geograph.org.uk_-_526488.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Moss-covered_grave,_St._Mary%27s,_Newent._-_geograph.org.uk_-_526488.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Moss-covered grave</div></div></div>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold">Moss green</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;line-height:12px; background-color:#8A9A5B; border: 0.1px solid #000000">
 </td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><span style="position: relative; float: right; font-size: 70%"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Color/Normalized_Color_Coordinates" title="About these coordinates"><img alt="About these coordinates" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="60" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/15px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/23px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/30px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 2x" width="15"/></a></span>     Color coordinates</th></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Web_colors#Hex_triplet" title="Web colors">Hex triplet</a></th><td>
#8A9A5B</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/SRGB_color_space" title="SRGB color space">sRGB</a><sup><b>B</b></sup>  (<a href="/wiki/Red" title="Red">r</a>, <a href="/wiki/Green" title="Green">g</a>, <a href="/wiki/Blue" title="Blue">b</a>)</th><td>

<span class="nowrap">(10, 0, 41, 40)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HSV_color_space" title="HSV color space">HSV</a>       (<a href="/wiki/Hue" title="Hue">h</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saturation_(color_theory)" title="Saturation (color theory)">s</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brightness" title="Brightness">v</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(75°, 41%, 60%)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Source</th><td>
<a class="external text" href="http://tx4.us/nbs/nbs-m.htm" rel="nofollow">ISCC NBS</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/><b>H</b>: Normalized to [0–100] (hundred)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><i>Moss green</i> is a tone of green that resembles <a href="/wiki/Moss" title="Moss">moss</a>.
</p><p>The first recorded use of <i>moss green</i> as a color name in English was in 1884.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19"><a href="#cite_note-19">[19]</a></sup>
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Myrtle_green">Myrtle green</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Myrtle green">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold">Myrtle green</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;line-height:12px; background-color:#317873; border: 0.1px solid #000000">
 </td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><span style="position: relative; float: right; font-size: 70%"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Color/Normalized_Color_Coordinates" title="About these coordinates"><img alt="About these coordinates" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="60" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/15px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/23px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/30px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 2x" width="15"/></a></span>     Color coordinates</th></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Web_colors#Hex_triplet" title="Web colors">Hex triplet</a></th><td>
#317873</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/SRGB_color_space" title="SRGB color space">sRGB</a><sup><b>B</b></sup>  (<a href="/wiki/Red" title="Red">r</a>, <a href="/wiki/Green" title="Green">g</a>, <a href="/wiki/Blue" title="Blue">b</a>)</th><td>
(49, 120, 115)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/CMYK_color_model" title="CMYK color model">CMYK</a><sup><b>H</b></sup>   (<a href="/wiki/Cyan" title="Cyan">c</a>, <a href="/wiki/Magenta" title="Magenta">m</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yellow" title="Yellow">y</a>, <a href="/wiki/Black" title="Black">k</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(59, 0, 4, 53)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HSV_color_space" title="HSV color space">HSV</a>       (<a href="/wiki/Hue" title="Hue">h</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saturation_(color_theory)" title="Saturation (color theory)">s</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brightness" title="Brightness">v</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(176°, 59%, 47%)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Source</th><td>
<a class="external text" href="http://tx4.us/nbs/nbs-m.htm" rel="nofollow">ISCC NBS</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20"><a href="#cite_note-20">[20]</a></sup></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/><b>H</b>: Normalized to [0–100] (hundred)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><i>Myrtle green</i>, also called <i>myrtle</i>, is a color which is a representation of the color of the leaves of the <a href="/wiki/Myrtus" title="Myrtus">myrtle</a> plant.
</p><p>The first recorded use of <i>myrtle green</i> as a color name in English was in 1835.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21"><a href="#cite_note-21">[21]</a></sup>
</p><p><i>Myrtle</i> is the official designation of the green stripes on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Waterloo_R.F.C." title="Waterloo R.F.C.">Waterloo</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rugby_Union" title="Rugby Union">rugby</a> club's shirts, the green of <a href="/wiki/Hunslet_R.L.F.C." title="Hunslet R.L.F.C.">Hunslet</a>/<a href="/wiki/Hunslet_R.L.F.C." title="Hunslet R.L.F.C.">Hunslet</a> rugby league club, the green (along with the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cardinal_red" title="Cardinal red">cardinal red</a>) stripes of the <a href="/wiki/South_Sydney_Rabbitohs" title="South Sydney Rabbitohs">South Sydney Rabbitohs</a> and the green of the blazers, sports kit and scarf of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St._Aloysius%27_College,_Glasgow" title="St. Aloysius' College, Glasgow">St. Aloysius' College, Glasgow</a>. It is also one of the school colors of <a href="/wiki/Lane_Technical_College_Prep_High_School" title="Lane Technical College Prep High School">Lane Technical College Prep High School</a> in Chicago, the other being <a href="/wiki/Gold_(color)#Old_gold" title="Gold (color)">old gold</a>.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Aniseed_myrtle.JPG"><img alt="Aniseed myrtle" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2304" data-file-width="3072" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/68/Aniseed_myrtle.JPG/220px-Aniseed_myrtle.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/68/Aniseed_myrtle.JPG/330px-Aniseed_myrtle.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/68/Aniseed_myrtle.JPG/440px-Aniseed_myrtle.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Aniseed_myrtle.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Aniseed_myrtle" title="Aniseed myrtle">Aniseed myrtle</a></div></div></div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Baggy_green" title="Baggy green">baggy green</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Cricket_cap" title="Cricket cap">cricket cap</a> worn by Australian <a href="/wiki/Test_cricket" title="Test cricket">Test cricketers</a> since around the turn of the twentieth century, is <i>myrtle green</i> in color.
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pine_green">Pine green</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Pine green">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Spring_green#Pine_green" title="Spring green">Spring green § Pine green</a></div>

 </td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><span style="position: relative; float: right; font-size: 70%"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Color/Normalized_Color_Coordinates" title="About these coordinates"><img alt="About these coordinates" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="60" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/15px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/23px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/30px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 2x" width="15"/></a></span>     Color coordinates</th></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Web_colors#Hex_triplet" title="Web colors">Hex triplet</a></th><td>

<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/><b>H</b>: Normalized to [0–100] (hundred)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><i>Pine green</i> is a rich shade of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Spring_green_(color)" title="Spring green (color)">spring green</a> that resembles the color of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pine_tree" title="Pine tree">pine trees</a>. It is an official Crayola color (since 1903).<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (October 2017)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Pine_tree_(6132312936).jpg"><img alt="A small pine tree" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3888" data-file-width="2592" height="330" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b7/Pine_tree_%286132312936%29.jpg/220px-Pine_tree_%286132312936%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b7/Pine_tree_%286132312936%29.jpg/330px-Pine_tree_%286132312936%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b7/Pine_tree_%286132312936%29.jpg/440px-Pine_tree_%286132312936%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Pine_tree_(6132312936).jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>A small pine tree</div></div></div>
<p>The first recorded use of <i>pine tree</i> as a color name in English was in 1923.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22"><a href="#cite_note-22">[22]</a></sup>
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>

<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Wild_Mignonette_(Reseda_lutea).jpg"><img alt="Wild mignonette" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1785" data-file-width="2379" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/46/Wild_Mignonette_%28Reseda_lutea%29.jpg/220px-Wild_Mignonette_%28Reseda_lutea%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/46/Wild_Mignonette_%28Reseda_lutea%29.jpg/330px-Wild_Mignonette_%28Reseda_lutea%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/46/Wild_Mignonette_%28Reseda_lutea%29.jpg/440px-Wild_Mignonette_%28Reseda_lutea%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Wild_Mignonette_(Reseda_lutea).jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Wild <a href="/wiki/Reseda_(plant)" title="Reseda (plant)">mignonette</a></div></div></div>
<p>Reseda green is a shade of greyish green in the classic range of colours of the German <a href="/wiki/RAL_colour_standard" title="RAL colour standard">RAL colour standard</a>, where it is colour 6011.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23"><a href="#cite_note-23">[23]</a></sup> The name derives from the colour of the leaves of <i><a href="/wiki/Reseda_odorata" title="Reseda odorata">Reseda odorata</a></i>, commonly known as mignonette.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nik_24-0"><a href="#cite_note-nik-24">[24]</a></sup>
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sap_green">Sap green</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Sap green">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><i>Sap green</i> is a green pigment that was traditionally made of ripe <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Buckthorn" title="Buckthorn">buckthorn</a> berries.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Vergnaud1874_25-0"><a href="#cite_note-Vergnaud1874-25">[25]</a></sup> However, modern colors marketed under this name are usually a blend of other pigments, commonly with a basis of <a href="/wiki/Phthalocyanine_Green_G" title="Phthalocyanine Green G">Phthalocyanine Green G</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MacEvoy2018_26-0"><a href="#cite_note-MacEvoy2018-26">[26]</a></sup> Sap green paint was frequently used on <a href="/wiki/Bob_Ross" title="Bob Ross">Bob Ross</a>' <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Television_program" title="Television program">TV show</a>, <i><a href="/wiki/The_Joy_of_Painting" title="The Joy of Painting">The Joy of Painting</a></i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bobross_27-0"><a href="#cite_note-bobross-27">[27]</a></sup>
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span id="Shamrock_green_.28Irish_green.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Shamrock_green_(Irish_green)"><span id="Shamrock_green"></span> Shamrock green (Irish green)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Shamrock green (Irish green)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold">Shamrock green</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;line-height:12px; background-color:#009E60; border: 0.1px solid #000000">
 </td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center">Common connotations</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St._Patrick%27s_Day" title="St. Patrick's Day">St. Patrick's Day</a></td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><span style="position: relative; float: right; font-size: 70%"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Color/Normalized_Color_Coordinates" title="About these coordinates"><img alt="About these coordinates" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="60" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/15px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/23px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/30px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 2x" width="15"/></a></span>     Color coordinates</th></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Web_colors#Hex_triplet" title="Web colors">Hex triplet</a></th><td>
#009E60</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/SRGB_color_space" title="SRGB color space">sRGB</a><sup><b>B</b></sup>  (<a href="/wiki/Red" title="Red">r</a>, <a href="/wiki/Green" title="Green">g</a>, <a href="/wiki/Blue" title="Blue">b</a>)</th><td>
(0, 158, 96)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/CMYK_color_model" title="CMYK color model">CMYK</a><sup><b>H</b></sup>   (<a href="/wiki/Cyan" title="Cyan">c</a>, <a href="/wiki/Magenta" title="Magenta">m</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yellow" title="Yellow">y</a>, <a href="/wiki/Black" title="Black">k</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(100, 0, 86, 3)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HSV_color_space" title="HSV color space">HSV</a>       (<a href="/wiki/Hue" title="Hue">h</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saturation_(color_theory)" title="Saturation (color theory)">s</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brightness" title="Brightness">v</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(156°, 100%, 62%)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Source</th><td>
Maerz and Paul<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28"><a href="#cite_note-28">[28]</a></sup></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/><b>H</b>: Normalized to [0–100] (hundred)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><i>Shamrock green</i> is a tone of green that represents the color of <a href="/wiki/Shamrock" title="Shamrock">shamrocks</a>, a symbol of Ireland.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29"><a href="#cite_note-29">[29]</a></sup>
</p><p>The first recorded use of <i>shamrock</i> as a color name in English was in the 1820s (exact year uncertain).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30"><a href="#cite_note-30">[30]</a></sup>
</p><p>This green is also defined as <i>Irish green</i> <a href="/wiki/Pantone" title="Pantone">Pantone</a> 347.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31"><a href="#cite_note-31">[31]</a></sup>
</p><p>This green is used as the green on the <a href="/wiki/Flag_of_Ireland" title="Flag of Ireland">national flag</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">Republic of Ireland</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32"><a href="#cite_note-32">[32]</a></sup>
</p><p>It is customary in Ireland, Australia, New Zealand, Canada and the United States to wear this or any other tone of green on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St._Patrick%27s_Day" title="St. Patrick's Day">St. Patrick's Day</a>, March 17.
</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">State of California</a> uses this shade of green of the grass under the bear on their <a href="/wiki/Flag_of_California" title="Flag of California">state flag</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33"><a href="#cite_note-33">[33]</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Shamrock_leaves.jpg"><img alt="Shamrocks" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1536" data-file-width="2560" height="132" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Shamrock_leaves.jpg/220px-Shamrock_leaves.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Shamrock_leaves.jpg/330px-Shamrock_leaves.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Shamrock_leaves.jpg/440px-Shamrock_leaves.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Shamrock_leaves.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Shamrock" title="Shamrock">Shamrocks</a></div></div></div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Boston_Celtics" title="Boston Celtics">Boston Celtics</a> of the <a href="/wiki/National_Basketball_Association" title="National Basketball Association">National Basketball Association</a> use this shade for their uniforms, logos and other memorabilia.
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tea_green">Tea green</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Tea green">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold">Tea green</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;line-height:12px; background-color:#D0F0C0; border: 0.1px solid #000000">
 </td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><span style="position: relative; float: right; font-size: 70%"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Color/Normalized_Color_Coordinates" title="About these coordinates"><img alt="About these coordinates" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="60" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/15px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/23px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/30px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 2x" width="15"/></a></span>     Color coordinates</th></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Web_colors#Hex_triplet" title="Web colors">Hex triplet</a></th><td>
#D0F0C0</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/SRGB_color_space" title="SRGB color space">sRGB</a><sup><b>B</b></sup>  (<a href="/wiki/Red" title="Red">r</a>, <a href="/wiki/Green" title="Green">g</a>, <a href="/wiki/Blue" title="Blue">b</a>)</th><td>
(208, 240, 192)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/CMYK_color_model" title="CMYK color model">CMYK</a><sup><b>H</b></sup>   (<a href="/wiki/Cyan" title="Cyan">c</a>, <a href="/wiki/Magenta" title="Magenta">m</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yellow" title="Yellow">y</a>, <a href="/wiki/Black" title="Black">k</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(13, 0, 20, 6)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HSV_color_space" title="HSV color space">HSV</a>       (<a href="/wiki/Hue" title="Hue">h</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saturation_(color_theory)" title="Saturation (color theory)">s</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brightness" title="Brightness">v</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(100°, 20%, 94%)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Source</th><td>
<a class="external text" href="http://encycolorpedia.com/d0f0c0" rel="nofollow">Encycolorpedia</a></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/><b>H</b>: Normalized to [0–100] (hundred)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">"Tea Green" redirects here. For the hamlet near Luton, see <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tea_Green,_Hertfordshire" title="Tea Green, Hertfordshire">Tea Green, Hertfordshire</a>.</div>
<p><i>Tea green</i> is a light shade of green. It is a representation of the color of brewed <a href="/wiki/Green_tea" title="Green tea">green tea</a>, i.e., the color of the hot green tea after the green tea leaves have been brewed in boiling water.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34"><a href="#cite_note-34">[34]</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Iced_green_tea_and_dango.jpg"><img alt="Iced green tea with dango" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="480" data-file-width="640" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Iced_green_tea_and_dango.jpg/220px-Iced_green_tea_and_dango.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Iced_green_tea_and_dango.jpg/330px-Iced_green_tea_and_dango.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Iced_green_tea_and_dango.jpg/440px-Iced_green_tea_and_dango.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Iced_green_tea_and_dango.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Iced <a href="/wiki/Green_tea" title="Green tea">green tea</a> with <a href="/wiki/Dango" title="Dango">dango</a></div></div></div>
<p>The first recorded use of <i>tea green</i> as a color name in English was in 1858.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35"><a href="#cite_note-35">[35]</a></sup>
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>

<p><i>Teal</i> is displayed at right. It is a dark <a href="/wiki/Cyan" title="Cyan">cyan</a> color that is a representation of the color of the neck coloring of a duck called the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Common_teal" title="Common teal">common teal</a>.
</p>

<p>Olive is the shade of dark yellow-green found on green <a href="/wiki/Olive" title="Olive">olives</a>. It has been commonly used by militaries around the world as a color for uniforms and equipment.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Computer_web_color_greens">Computer web color greens</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Computer web color greens">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Green">Green</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Green">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span id="X11_green"></span>
</p>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold">Green (X11, color wheel)</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;line-height:12px; background-color:#00FF00; border: 0.1px solid #000000">
 </td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><span style="position: relative; float: right; font-size: 70%"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Color/Normalized_Color_Coordinates" title="About these coordinates"><img alt="About these coordinates" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="60" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/15px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/23px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/30px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 2x" width="15"/></a></span>     Color coordinates</th></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Web_colors#Hex_triplet" title="Web colors">Hex triplet</a></th><td>
#00FF00</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/SRGB_color_space" title="SRGB color space">sRGB</a><sup><b>B</b></sup>  (<a href="/wiki/Red" title="Red">r</a>, <a href="/wiki/Green" title="Green">g</a>, <a href="/wiki/Blue" title="Blue">b</a>)</th><td>
(00, 255, 00)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/CMYK_color_model" title="CMYK color model">CMYK</a><sup><b>H</b></sup>   (<a href="/wiki/Cyan" title="Cyan">c</a>, <a href="/wiki/Magenta" title="Magenta">m</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yellow" title="Yellow">y</a>, <a href="/wiki/Black" title="Black">k</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(100, 0, 100, 0)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HSV_color_space" title="HSV color space">HSV</a>       (<a href="/wiki/Hue" title="Hue">h</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saturation_(color_theory)" title="Saturation (color theory)">s</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brightness" title="Brightness">v</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(120°, 100%, 100%)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Source</th><td>
<a href="/wiki/X11_color_names" title="X11 color names">X11 color names</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37"><a href="#cite_note-37">[37]</a></sup><br/><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HTML_color_names" title="HTML color names">HTML/CSS</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-css3-color_1-4"><a href="#cite_note-css3-color-1">[1]</a></sup></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/><b>H</b>: Normalized to [0–100] (hundred)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:142px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:RGB_illumination.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="300" data-file-width="400" height="105" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/RGB_illumination.jpg/140px-RGB_illumination.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/RGB_illumination.jpg/210px-RGB_illumination.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/RGB_illumination.jpg/280px-RGB_illumination.jpg 2x" width="140"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:RGB_illumination.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Red, green and blue lights, representing the three basic <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Additive_primary" title="Additive primary">additive primary</a> colors of the RGB color system, red, green, and blue.</div></div></div>
<p>The color defined as <i>green</i> in the <a href="/wiki/RGB_color_model" title="RGB color model">RGB color model</a>, displayed on the right, is the brightest possible green that can be reproduced on a computer screen, and is the color named <i>green</i> in <a href="/wiki/X11_color_names" title="X11 color names">X11</a>. It is one of the three <a href="/wiki/Primary_color" title="Primary color">primary colors</a> used in the <a href="/wiki/RGB_color_space" title="RGB color space">RGB color space</a> along with <a href="/wiki/Red" title="Red">red</a> and <a href="/wiki/Blue" title="Blue">blue</a>. The three additive primaries in the RGB color system are the three colors of light chosen such as to provide the maximum range of colors that are capable of being represented on a computer or television set.
</p><p>This color is also called <i>regular green</i>. It is at precisely 120 degrees on the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HSV_color_space" title="HSV color space">HSV color wheel</a>, also known as the RGB color wheel (<a href="/wiki/File:RBG_color_wheel.svg" title="File:RBG color wheel.svg">Image of RGB color wheel</a>). Its <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Complementary_color" title="Complementary color">complementary color</a> is <a href="/wiki/Magenta" title="Magenta">magenta</a>.
</p><p>Another name for this color is <i>green</i> as opposed to the darker <i>HTML/CSS green</i> and the deeper <i>pigment green</i>, both shown below.
</p><p>Green takes up a large portion of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/CIE_chromaticity_diagram" title="CIE chromaticity diagram">CIE chromaticity diagram</a> because it is in the central area of human color perception.
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>

(0, 128, 0)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/CMYK_color_model" title="CMYK color model">CMYK</a><sup><b>H</b></sup>   (<a href="/wiki/Cyan" title="Cyan">c</a>, <a href="/wiki/Magenta" title="Magenta">m</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yellow" title="Yellow">y</a>, <a href="/wiki/Black" title="Black">k</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(100, 0, 100, 50)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HSV_color_space" title="HSV color space">HSV</a>       (<a href="/wiki/Hue" title="Hue">h</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saturation_(color_theory)" title="Saturation (color theory)">s</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brightness" title="Brightness">v</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(120°, 100%, 50%)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Source</th><td>
<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HTML_color_names" title="HTML color names">HTML/CSS</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-css3-color_1-5"><a href="#cite_note-css3-color-1">[1]</a></sup></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/><b>H</b>: Normalized to [0–100] (hundred)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>The color defined as <i>green</i> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HTML_color_names" title="HTML color names">HTML/CSS</a> color standard is displayed at right. It is the color called green, low green or medium green in many of the older <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_8-bit_computer_hardware_palettes" title="List of 8-bit computer hardware palettes">eight-bit computer palettes</a>.
</p><p>Another name for this color is <i>green <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/W3C" title="W3C">W3C</a></i>.
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
