<p><i>Midnight green</i> (sometimes called <i>Eagle green</i>) is the official primary color of the <a href="/wiki/Philadelphia_Eagles" title="Philadelphia Eagles">Philadelphia Eagles</a> of the National Football League.
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="MSU_green">MSU green</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=60" title="Edit section: MSU green">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold">MSU green</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;line-height:12px; background-color:#18453B; border: 0.1px solid #000000">
 </td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><span style="position: relative; float: right; font-size: 70%"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Color/Normalized_Color_Coordinates" title="About these coordinates"><img alt="About these coordinates" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="60" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/15px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/23px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/30px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 2x" width="15"/></a></span>     Color coordinates</th></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Web_colors#Hex_triplet" title="Web colors">Hex triplet</a></th><td>
#18453B</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/SRGB_color_space" title="SRGB color space">sRGB</a><sup><b>B</b></sup>  (<a href="/wiki/Red" title="Red">r</a>, <a href="/wiki/Green" title="Green">g</a>, <a href="/wiki/Blue" title="Blue">b</a>)</th><td>
(24, 69, 59)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/CMYK_color_model" title="CMYK color model">CMYK</a><sup><b>H</b></sup>   (<a href="/wiki/Cyan" title="Cyan">c</a>, <a href="/wiki/Magenta" title="Magenta">m</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yellow" title="Yellow">y</a>, <a href="/wiki/Black" title="Black">k</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(82, 0, 64, 70)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HSV_color_space" title="HSV color space">HSV</a>       (<a href="/wiki/Hue" title="Hue">h</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saturation_(color_theory)" title="Saturation (color theory)">s</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brightness" title="Brightness">v</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(111°, 116%, 44%)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Source</th><td>
<a class="external text" href="http://brand.msu.edu/design-visual/index.html#color" rel="nofollow">Brand Guide</a></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/><b>H</b>: Normalized to [0–100] (hundred)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>Green and white are the primary school colors representing <a href="/wiki/Michigan_State_University" title="Michigan State University">Michigan State University</a>. The university <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Board_of_trustees" title="Board of trustees">board of trustees</a> officially standardized MSU green as part of a larger university branding effort, replacing a lighter green (PMS 341) used from 1997–2010. The official color was chosen based on the traditional darker Spartan green found on the original university varsity letter jackets and marching band jackets. The official green of Michigan State University is represented by Pantone Matching System ink color 567 (PMS 567).
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>

</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pakistan_green">Pakistan green</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=63" title="Edit section: Pakistan green">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold">Pakistan green</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;line-height:12px; background-color:#006600; border: 0.1px solid #000000">
 </td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><span style="position: relative; float: right; font-size: 70%"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Color/Normalized_Color_Coordinates" title="About these coordinates"><img alt="About these coordinates" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="60" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/15px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/23px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/30px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 2x" width="15"/></a></span>     Color coordinates</th></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Web_colors#Hex_triplet" title="Web colors">Hex triplet</a></th><td>

(0, 102, 0)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HSV_color_space" title="HSV color space">HSV</a>       (<a href="/wiki/Hue" title="Hue">h</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saturation_(color_theory)" title="Saturation (color theory)">s</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brightness" title="Brightness">v</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(120°, 100%, 40%)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Source</th><td>
<sup>[<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Color/Sources_for_Color_Coordinates" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Color/Sources for Color Coordinates">Unsourced</a>]</sup></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><i>Pakistan green</i> is a shade of dark green, used in web development and graphic design. It is also the background color of the <a href="/wiki/Flag_of_Pakistan" title="Flag of Pakistan">Flag of Pakistan</a>. It is almost identical to the HTML/<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/X11" title="X11">X11</a> <a href="/wiki/Shades_of_green#Dark_green_(X11)" title="Shades of green">dark green</a> in <a href="/wiki/SRGB" title="SRGB">sRGB</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HSV_color_space" title="HSV color space">HSV</a> values.
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Paris_green">Paris green</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=64" title="Edit section: Paris green">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<p><i>Paris green</i> is a color that ranges from pale and vivid blue green to deeper true green. It comes from the <a href="/wiki/Inorganic_compound" title="Inorganic compound">inorganic compound</a> copper (II) acetoarsenite and was once a popular pigment in artists' paints.
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>

<p><i>Persian green</i> is a color used in <a href="/wiki/Persian_pottery" title="Persian pottery">Persian pottery</a> and <a href="/wiki/Persian_carpet" title="Persian carpet">Persian carpets</a> in Iran.
</p><p>The first recorded use of <i>Persian green</i> as a color name in English was in 1892.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-78"><a href="#cite_note-78">[78]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-79"><a href="#cite_note-79">[79]</a></sup>
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Rifle_green">Rifle green</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=66" title="Edit section: Rifle green">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold">Rifle green</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;line-height:12px; background-color:#444C38; border: 0.1px solid #000000">
 </td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><span style="position: relative; float: right; font-size: 70%"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Color/Normalized_Color_Coordinates" title="About these coordinates"><img alt="About these coordinates" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="60" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/15px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/23px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/30px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 2x" width="15"/></a></span>     Color coordinates</th></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Web_colors#Hex_triplet" title="Web colors">Hex triplet</a></th><td>

<span class="nowrap">(84°, 26%, 30%)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Source</th><td>

<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:US_President_JF_Kennedy_inspects_Bermuda_Rifles_1961.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="999" data-file-width="1000" height="220" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/US_President_JF_Kennedy_inspects_Bermuda_Rifles_1961.jpg/220px-US_President_JF_Kennedy_inspects_Bermuda_Rifles_1961.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/US_President_JF_Kennedy_inspects_Bermuda_Rifles_1961.jpg/330px-US_President_JF_Kennedy_inspects_Bermuda_Rifles_1961.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/US_President_JF_Kennedy_inspects_Bermuda_Rifles_1961.jpg/440px-US_President_JF_Kennedy_inspects_Bermuda_Rifles_1961.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:US_President_JF_Kennedy_inspects_Bermuda_Rifles_1961.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/John_Fitzgerald_Kennedy" title="John Fitzgerald Kennedy">John Fitzgerald Kennedy</a>, escorted by a <a href="/wiki/Bermuda_Militia_Artillery" title="Bermuda Militia Artillery">Bermuda Militia Artillery</a> officer in <a href="/wiki/Royal_Artillery" title="Royal Artillery">Royal Artillery</a> blue No. 1 dress, inspects green-uniformed riflemen of the <a href="/wiki/Bermuda_Volunteer_Rifle_Corps" title="Bermuda Volunteer Rifle Corps">Bermuda Rifles</a> in 1961</div></div></div>
<p>The color <i>rifle green</i> is displayed at right.
</p><p>The source of this color is the Pantone Textile Paper eXtended (TPX) color list, color No. 19-0419 TPX—Rifle green.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-82"><a href="#cite_note-82">[82]</a></sup>
</p><p>The first recorded use of <i>rifle green</i> as a color name in English was in 1858.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-83"><a href="#cite_note-83">[83]</a></sup>
</p><p>Rifle green is so named from the distinctive color of the uniform of rifle regiments (a form of <a href="/wiki/Light_infantry" title="Light infantry">light infantry</a>) of a number of European armies, and is still used as such by rifle regiments in many <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_of_Nations" title="Commonwealth of Nations">Commonwealth</a> armies, such as <a href="/wiki/The_Rifles" title="The Rifles">the Rifles</a> and <a href="/wiki/Royal_Gurkha_Rifles" title="Royal Gurkha Rifles">Royal Gurkha Rifles</a> of the <a href="/wiki/British_Army" title="British Army">British Army</a> and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Queen%27s_Own_Rifles_of_Canada" title="Queen's Own Rifles of Canada">Queen's Own Rifles of Canada</a>.
</p><p>Rifle green was originally adopted by rifle regiments in the 18th century, including the famous <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/95th_Rifles" title="95th Rifles">95th Rifles</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Napoleonic_Wars" title="Napoleonic Wars">Napoleonic Wars</a>. As the traditional role of riflemen was that of <a href="/wiki/Marksman" title="Marksman">marksmen</a> and <a href="/wiki/Skirmisher" title="Skirmisher">skirmishers</a> who attacked behind the cover of trees, a dark green uniform was adopted as an early form of <a href="/wiki/Camouflage" title="Camouflage">camouflage</a>, as opposed to the colorful uniforms worn by other soldiers of the period. The vegetable based dyes used during the 18th and early 19th centuries were not <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Color_fastness" title="Color fastness">fast</a>, frequently fading after exposure to the elements to lighter shades of green or even brown. While this had advantages in terms of reduced visibility on active service, it did not make for a smart appearance on the peace-time parade ground. Accordingly, the color of the rifleman's uniform was progressively darkened until it approached black. After 1890 the development of chemical dyes permitted the adoption of the stable shade of rifle green now worn. In the U.S. armed forces, the green beret may be worn only by soldiers awarded the Special Forces Tab, signifying they have been qualified as special forces soldiers. The special forces beret is officially designated "beret, man's, wool, rifle green, army shade 297". Previously, rifle green uniforms had been issued to <a href="/wiki/Hiram_Berdan" title="Hiram Berdan">Hiram Berdan</a>'s elite <a href="/wiki/1st_United_States_Sharpshooters" title="1st United States Sharpshooters">1st United States Sharpshooters</a> and <a href="/wiki/2nd_United_States_Sharpshooters" title="2nd United States Sharpshooters">2nd United States Sharpshooters</a> during the <a href="/wiki/American_Civil_War" title="American Civil War">American Civil War</a>.
</p><p>Rifle green was the official uniform color of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Canadian_Forces" title="Canadian Forces">Canadian Forces</a> (CF) after unification; it was thereafter generally referred to as "CF green"; indeed, the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Service_dress" title="Service dress">service dress</a> uniform of the day was referred to as "CF greens". After the introduction of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Uniforms_of_the_Canadian_Forces#Distinct_Environmental_Uniform" title="Uniforms of the Canadian Forces">distinct environmental uniform</a> (DEU), rifle green remained as the uniform color of the winter land environment DEU; a short-lived tan uniform was worn in summer. After the demise of the tans, the rifle green DEU was worn year-round. Rifle green was also the color of the uniform worn by the Northern Irish <a href="/wiki/Royal_Ulster_Constabulary" title="Royal Ulster Constabulary">Royal Ulster Constabulary</a> (RUC) until 2001 where the RUC was renamed the <a href="/wiki/Police_Service_of_Northern_Ireland" title="Police Service of Northern Ireland">PSNI</a> and while the uniform color remained the same, terminology changed to "<a href="/wiki/Shades_of_green#Bottle_green" title="Shades of green">bottle green</a>".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-84"><a href="#cite_note-84">[84]</a></sup>
</p><p>Rifle green is 19–0419 TPX in the Pantone palette, or hex code #444C38 in the <a href="/wiki/SRGB" title="SRGB">sRGB</a> color space, as shown above.
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>

<p>The color <i>Russian green</i> is displayed at right.
</p><p>The first recorded use of <i>Russian green</i> as a color name in English was in the 1830s (exact year uncertain).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-86"><a href="#cite_note-86">[86]</a></sup> The term appears to refer to the medium shade of green worn by most regiments of the Imperial Russian Army from 1700 to 1914.
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sacramento_State_green">Sacramento State green</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=68" title="Edit section: Sacramento State green">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold">Sacramento State green</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;line-height:12px; background-color:#043927; border: 0.1px solid #000000">
 </td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><span style="position: relative; float: right; font-size: 70%"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Color/Normalized_Color_Coordinates" title="About these coordinates"><img alt="About these coordinates" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="60" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/15px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/23px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/30px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 2x" width="15"/></a></span>     Color coordinates</th></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Web_colors#Hex_triplet" title="Web colors">Hex triplet</a></th><td>

<span class="nowrap">(164°, 100%, 34%)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Source</th><td>
<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CSUS_87-0"><a href="#cite_note-CSUS-87">[87]</a></sup></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/><b>H</b>: Normalized to [0–100] (hundred)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>In 2004, <a href="/wiki/California_State_University,_Sacramento" title="California State University, Sacramento">California State University, Sacramento</a> rebranded itself as Sacramento State, while keeping the official name as the long form. In the process of rebranding a new logo was selected, and in 2005 it formalized the colors which it would use.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CSUS_87-1"><a href="#cite_note-CSUS-87">[87]</a></sup>
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span id="Screamin.27_green"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Screamin'_green">Screamin' green</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=69" title="Edit section: Screamin' green">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold">Screamin' green</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;line-height:12px; background-color:#76FF7A; border: 0.1px solid #000000">
 </td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><span style="position: relative; float: right; font-size: 70%"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Color/Normalized_Color_Coordinates" title="About these coordinates"><img alt="About these coordinates" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="60" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/15px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/23px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/30px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 2x" width="15"/></a></span>     Color coordinates</th></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Web_colors#Hex_triplet" title="Web colors">Hex triplet</a></th><td>
#76FF7A</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/SRGB_color_space" title="SRGB color space">sRGB</a><sup><b>B</b></sup>  (<a href="/wiki/Red" title="Red">r</a>, <a href="/wiki/Green" title="Green">g</a>, <a href="/wiki/Blue" title="Blue">b</a>)</th><td>
(118, 255, 122)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/CMYK_color_model" title="CMYK color model">CMYK</a><sup><b>H</b></sup>   (<a href="/wiki/Cyan" title="Cyan">c</a>, <a href="/wiki/Magenta" title="Magenta">m</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yellow" title="Yellow">y</a>, <a href="/wiki/Black" title="Black">k</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(137, 0, 133, 0)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HSV_color_space" title="HSV color space">HSV</a>       (<a href="/wiki/Hue" title="Hue">h</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saturation_(color_theory)" title="Saturation (color theory)">s</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brightness" title="Brightness">v</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(156°, 100%, 62%)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Source</th><td>
Crayola</td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/><b>H</b>: Normalized to [0–100] (hundred)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>The color <i>screamin' green</i> is shown at right.
</p><p>This color was renamed from <i>ultra green</i> by Crayola in 1990.
</p><p>This color is a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fluorescent" title="Fluorescent">fluorescent</a> color.
</p>

<table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold">Sea green</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;line-height:12px; background-color:#2E8B57; border: 0.1px solid #000000">
 </td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><span style="position: relative; float: right; font-size: 70%"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Color/Normalized_Color_Coordinates" title="About these coordinates"><img alt="About these coordinates" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="60" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/15px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/23px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/30px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 2x" width="15"/></a></span>     Color coordinates</th></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Web_colors#Hex_triplet" title="Web colors">Hex triplet</a></th><td>

<span class="nowrap">(146°, 67%, 55%)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Source</th><td>

<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/><b>H</b>: Normalized to [0–100] (hundred)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><i>Sea green</i> is a color that resembles the <a href="/wiki/Seabed" title="Seabed">sea floor</a> as seen from the surface.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="SGBUS_green">SGBUS green</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=71" title="Edit section: SGBUS green">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold">SGBUS green</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;line-height:12px; background-color:#55dd33; border: 0.1px solid #000000">
 </td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><span style="position: relative; float: right; font-size: 70%"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Color/Normalized_Color_Coordinates" title="About these coordinates"><img alt="About these coordinates" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="60" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/15px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/23px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/30px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 2x" width="15"/></a></span>     Color coordinates</th></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Web_colors#Hex_triplet" title="Web colors">Hex triplet</a></th><td>

(85, 221, 51)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/CMYK_color_model" title="CMYK color model">CMYK</a><sup><b>H</b></sup>   (<a href="/wiki/Cyan" title="Cyan">c</a>, <a href="/wiki/Magenta" title="Magenta">m</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yellow" title="Yellow">y</a>, <a href="/wiki/Black" title="Black">k</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(61.5, 0, 76.9, 13.3)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HSV_color_space" title="HSV color space">HSV</a>       (<a href="/wiki/Hue" title="Hue">h</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saturation_(color_theory)" title="Saturation (color theory)">s</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brightness" title="Brightness">v</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(108°, 76.9%, 86.7%)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Source</th><td>
<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HTML_color_names" title="HTML color names">HTML/CSS</a></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/><b>H</b>: Normalized to [0–100] (hundred)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><i>SGBUS green</i> is the color voted by the public and used by <a href="/wiki/Land_Transport_Authority" title="Land Transport Authority">Singapore</a> to colour all its government-owned public buses.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-88"><a href="#cite_note-88">[88]</a></sup>
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Spanish_green">Spanish green</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=72" title="Edit section: Spanish green">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold">Green (G&amp;S)</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;line-height:12px; background-color:#009150; border: 0.1px solid #000000">
 </td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><span style="position: relative; float: right; font-size: 70%"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Color/Normalized_Color_Coordinates" title="About these coordinates"><img alt="About these coordinates" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="60" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/15px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/23px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/30px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 2x" width="15"/></a></span>     Color coordinates</th></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Web_colors#Hex_triplet" title="Web colors">Hex triplet</a></th><td>
#009150</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/SRGB_color_space" title="SRGB color space">sRGB</a><sup><b>B</b></sup>  (<a href="/wiki/Red" title="Red">r</a>, <a href="/wiki/Green" title="Green">g</a>, <a href="/wiki/Blue" title="Blue">b</a>)</th><td>
(0, 145, 80)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/CMYK_color_model" title="CMYK color model">CMYK</a><sup><b>H</b></sup>   (<a href="/wiki/Cyan" title="Cyan">c</a>, <a href="/wiki/Magenta" title="Magenta">m</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yellow" title="Yellow">y</a>, <a href="/wiki/Black" title="Black">k</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(100, 0, 100, 0)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HSV_color_space" title="HSV color space">HSV</a>       (<a href="/wiki/Hue" title="Hue">h</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saturation_(color_theory)" title="Saturation (color theory)">s</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brightness" title="Brightness">v</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(153°, 100%, 57%)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Source</th><td>
Gallego and Sanz<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-89"><a href="#cite_note-89">[89]</a></sup></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/><b>H</b>: Normalized to [0–100] (hundred)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><i>Spanish green</i> is the color that is called "<i>verde</i>" (the Spanish word for "green") in the <i>Guía de coloraciones</i> (<i>Guide to colorations</i>) by Rosa Gallego and
Juan Carlos Sanz, a color dictionary published in 2005 that is widely popular in the Hispanophone realm.
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="UNT_green">UNT green</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=73" title="Edit section: UNT green">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold">UNT green</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;line-height:12px; background-color:#00853E; border: 0.1px solid #000000">
 </td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><span style="position: relative; float: right; font-size: 70%"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Color/Normalized_Color_Coordinates" title="About these coordinates"><img alt="About these coordinates" data-file-height="60" data-file-width="60" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/15px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/23px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Gtk-dialog-info.svg/30px-Gtk-dialog-info.svg.png 2x" width="15"/></a></span>     Color coordinates</th></tr><tr><th scope="row"><a href="/wiki/Web_colors#Hex_triplet" title="Web colors">Hex triplet</a></th><td>

(5, 144, 51)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/CMYK_color_model" title="CMYK color model">CMYK</a><sup><b>H</b></sup>   (<a href="/wiki/Cyan" title="Cyan">c</a>, <a href="/wiki/Magenta" title="Magenta">m</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yellow" title="Yellow">y</a>, <a href="/wiki/Black" title="Black">k</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(98, 0, 95, 22)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HSV_color_space" title="HSV color space">HSV</a>       (<a href="/wiki/Hue" title="Hue">h</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saturation_(color_theory)" title="Saturation (color theory)">s</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brightness" title="Brightness">v</a>)</span></th><td>
<span class="nowrap">(93°, 224%, 70%)</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Source</th><td>
<a class="external text" href="https://identityguide.unt.edu/create-our-look/color" rel="nofollow">UNT Identity Guide</a></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<b>B</b>: Normalized to [0–255] (byte)<br/><b>H</b>: Normalized to [0–100] (hundred)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>UNT green is one of three official colors used by the University of North Texas. It is the primary color that appears on branding and promotional material produced by and on behalf of the university.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-90"><a href="#cite_note-90">[90]</a></sup>
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="UP_forest_green">UP forest green</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Shades_of_green&amp;action=edit&amp;section=74" title="Edit section: UP forest green">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<p>At the right is one of the official colors used by the <a href="/wiki/University_of_the_Philippines" title="University of the Philippines">University of the Philippines</a>, designated as "UP forest green". It is based on the approved color specifications to be used for the seal of the university.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-91"><a href="#cite_note-91">[91]</a></sup>
</p>
